Each journey traces the full lifecycle from first awareness through long-term retention, capturing user actions, system responses, emotional states, pain points, and platform opportunities at every step.

5 (Video upload) is the single highest drop-off risk in onboarding.

Show a &quot;How to record a great intro&quot; guide and allow unlimited re-records.

DELIGHT:  Approval email should feel like a congratulations letter, not a system notification.

Test deliverability from Nigerian mobile networks (MTN, Airtel) specifically.

INSIGHT:  Most Nigerian teachers will complete onboarding on Android mobile with variable internet.

All file uploads must show clear progress indicators and gracefully handle connection drops.

Every hour of unnecessary delay is lost supply and lost revenue.

DELIGHT:  The &quot;Request More Info&quot; path (Step 3.

1C) saves good teachers who submitted an imperfect first application.

Without it, every borderline applicant is rejected and lost permanently.

INSIGHT:  Admin rejection reason analytics (Step 4.

2) are a product feedback loop.

If 40% of teachers are rejected for poor video quality, the solution is better video guidance in onboarding, not more admin reviewers.
